msg:Traveling alone, I hesitated for a long time between Golden Eagle and Marriott before deciding on Golden Eagle. The following comments only represent my personal feelings.
1. The main entrance lacks the doorman and a**osphere that are required of high-star hotels. The only person standing at the door is not sure what he is doing (not helping with luggage, no welcome words). The fragrance at the entrance lacks representativeness. The lobby also coexists with other rentals. It is a bit downgraded.
2. The room is very good, and the cleaning is also very careful. The bedside, TV, elevator handrails, and windows at both ends of the corridor are basically dust-free. You can see that they are cleaned carefully every time.
3. I only used shampoo and shower gel for toiletries, which are too thin and feel like they are diluted with water.
4. Because it is of course hot when I check in, the air conditioner can't turn on the cold air. Because of the seasonality, it can be understood. (In fact, it doesn't cost much to equip the room with an air conditioner fan or air purifier).
5. The breakfast is a bit not worth the price (if you insist on counting the service charge, just ignore what I said), at least the small cake for breakfast on the first day tasted a strong refrigerator smell.
6. The front desk, cleaning and restaurant services are still in accordance with the standards, which is very good.
